The deadline was originally set for the end of last month. Now, because the number of smokers who have registered has been very enthusiastic, it is feared that some smokers have not been able to quit automatically. Therefore, out of consideration for the smokers, it has been specially approved by the Drug Prohibition Supervisor to extend the deadline for ten days, until the 10th of this month. This is the last opportunity for smokers in this city to register for a license or to quit drugs voluntarily. The Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a public notice to this effect yesterday. If they are found after the reporting deadline, they will be sent to the Songhu Garrison Command for severe punishment in accordance with the law, and no further extensions will be granted. Smokers must not delay and mislead themselves and fall into the legal net. The Municipal Public Security Bureau has ordered its subordinate branches and teams to step up house-to-house inspections in order to achieve complete success.

Rescue Information for the Jian Guo Vessel: Passengers Already Saved, Rescue to Commence After Unloading

As reported in yesterday's newspaper, the Jian Guo vessel of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ran aground on Qing Tian Reef in the Yangtze River. It is now known that the ship was traveling from Hankou to Shanghai when, at midnight on the 20th, a loud explosion occurred on board as the ship approached Qing Tian Reef downstream from Tongzhou. Upon hearing the explosion, the captain quickly inspected the ship and discovered that the steam pipe of the steering gear had suddenly burst, causing the rudder to break and the ship to lose steering control. At this time, the ship was battered by the current and, without stopping, drifted towards the shallows, resulting in the Jian Guo vessel

Becoming Grounded in the Shallows

When the ship ran aground, the bow was the first part to become stuck. The water depth at that location is eight feet at high tide, but the Jian Guo vessel's draft is eleven feet. Due to the damage to the steering gear, it was impossible to automatically refloat the ship. Yesterday morning, the company telegraphed the Jiang Shun vessel, which had been launched from Hankou, to go to the rescue. The Jiang Shun vessel arrived at approximately 8:00 AM, but could not proceed due to the low tide. Instead, it used sampans to transfer the more than one hundred passengers on board the Jian Guo vessel to the Jiang Shun, which then brought them to Shanghai. Shen Yougeng, the Jian Guo's purser, also came to Shanghai. The Jiang Shun departed at 9:30 AM and arrived in Shanghai at 4:15 PM in the afternoon, with all

Passengers Safely Arriving in Shanghai

They disembarked at the Jin Li Yuan Wharf. Yesterday morning, the company consulted with Jardine Matheson to charter the large tugboat Xue Po Xun, along with three large barges and a team of workers, to rush to Qing Quan Reef to rescue the Jian Guo vessel. Before the tugboat arrived, the company ordered the Jiang Hua vessel, which was traveling upstream, to also attempt a rescue and to bring food and coal to provide assistance. At approximately 6:00 PM last night, the company received a telegram from the owner of the Jiang Hua vessel stating that at 3:00 PM in the afternoon, during high tide (yesterday and today happened to be spring tides), the Jiang Hua vessel used a large steel cable to tow the Jian Guo vessel. The Jiang Hua vessel used full speed to attempt the rescue,

But After Three Hours

It was still unable to pull the ship out of the shallows. It has been determined that the Jian Guo vessel is thirty-one years old and was heavily loaded when it ran aground. If it were towed with great force, there would be a risk of damaging the hull, which would be a major problem. The Jiang Hua vessel stopped work and anchored on the river, waiting for the Xue Po Xun tugboat to arrive. It unloaded the coal and other supplies and then proceeded upstream to Hankou. It is estimated that the Jian Guo vessel will have 1,100 tons of cargo unloaded from its various holds by three barges to reduce the weight of the ship and allow it to float to the surface, as the Jian Guo vessel has a draft of only eight feet when empty. Then, the Xue Po Xun will tow it to Shanghai. According to the person in charge of cargo at the company, the Jian Guo vessel may be rescued this afternoon. Two warships from the Navy Department have already been dispatched to the area to

Protect the Vessel

The Jian Guo vessel is a regular passenger ship. However, because the company does not have any other Yangtze River vessels to send as a replacement, there will be no scheduled ship today. Even if the Jian Guo vessel is rescued and returned to Shanghai, it will need to undergo major repairs in the shipyard, which will be difficult to complete in a short period of time. The cost of hiring tugboats and barges, as well as the cost of repairs, will result in significant losses. After the Ministry of Finance's currency policy is implemented, the banknotes issued by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications are designated as legal tender. The banknotes issued by all commercial banks are to be taken over by the Issuance Reserve Management Committee, and no new banknotes are allowed to be issued. At the same time, the banknotes issued by the China Farmers Bank are specially authorized to be used in the same way as the legal tender of the three banks. Now, all commercial banks that issue banknotes have complied with the Ministry's order. However, all banks that have issued banknotes in the past can use 60% cash reserve and 40% guarantee reserve to obtain marked notes from the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and China Farmers Bank. For example, the marked notes that Zhejiang Industrial Bank obtains from the Bank of China are marked with the word "Yu" and can be used as usual. However, except for the three banks and the China Farmers Bank, the marked note methods of all banks that have issued banknotes in the past have been cancelled one after another.

Regulations for the Management of Coastal Merchant Ships and Shipping: Customs Notice on Amendments

Jianghai Customs Superintendent Zhu Changnian and Customs Commissioner Ba Runsen issued Notice No. 1543, stating that the amended regulations for the management of coastal merchant ships and shipping, which were announced in Notice No. 1400 on November 16, 1934, have been received from the Ministry of Finance with instructions to disseminate the amended Article 5 of the regulations for general knowledge. The amended article is listed below for the information of all merchant ship owners and captains. (Amended Article 5 of the Regulations for the Management of Coastal Merchant Ships and Shipping) All registered coastal merchant ships must re-register with the nearest Customs House or Customs post office every January. At the time of registration, they must first obtain an application form for the renewal of the navigation certificate and registration book for coastal merchant ships manufactured by the Customs House, fill it out item by item, sign and seal it by the ship owner or captain, and also find a merchant ship association, reputable shop, or bank to sign and seal the application form, guaranteeing that the ship owner or captain will strictly abide by all Customs regulations. If the provisions of this article are violated, the Customs House may confiscate the ship or fine the ship owner or captain up to 100 yuan in national currency, or confiscate the ship and impose a fine.

China Vegetable Oil Factory to Commence Operations in Mid-October: Interview with General Manager Zhang Jiazhu

The Ministry of Industry, in conjunction with the governments of Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, and Jiangxi provinces, as well as merchants from various provinces, has established the China Vegetable Oil Factory. The founding meeting was held in Guling on the 15th of last month, and Wu Dingchang and fifteen others were elected as directors, and Liu Yinful and six others were elected as supervisors. The first meeting of the board of directors and supervisors was held on the 17th, and Wu Dingchang was elected as chairman of the board, Zhou Yichun as vice chairman of the board, and Yu Jiezhu, Yang Liqian as standing directors, Wu Guozhen as standing supervisor, and the board of directors recommended Zhang Jiazhu as general manager and Lin Tianji as deputy general manager. It was also decided to establish six factories in Hankou, Shanghai, Changde, Changsha, Chongqing, and Wanxian, and Wu Jinquan, He Hu, Hu Ankai, Liu Hu and others were appointed as managers of each factory. After the meeting, they proceeded to establish the factories. General Manager Zhang returned to Shanghai a few days ago and told the Central News Agency reporter that the representatives from various provinces participated enthusiastically and harmoniously in the Guling meeting, and the progress of the project was very smooth. The factory's general office will be established in Hankou on the 15th of this month, and he will go there to preside over it. The six factories will be established first, and the factory managers have also been appointed to prepare for the establishment of the factories. Oil factories originally located in Hankou and Shanghai will be contacted for acquisition and operation, while the other locations will build their own buildings in order to gradually establish and start operations. Tung oil will be on the market in early January. This year, due to the good price of oil, farmers may harvest and press it earlier, so Shanghai, Hankou, and other places will start operations in mid-October as soon as possible.

The labor and management of the British-American Tobacco Company's Third Factory (renamed Gu Zhong Tobacco Company) on Tangpeng Road in Yangshupu in Shanghai have become increasingly polarized since the work slowdown began, and the dispute has not been resolved for more than ten days. The Party and government agencies have now decided to notify both labor and management to speak within a few days, and then form a mediation committee to formally conduct mediation.

Dancer Shi Lijuan Sues for Living Expenses: Defendant Fang Jiaheng Absent

Shi Lijuan, a former dancer from the Vienna Dance Hall and a native of Yixing, is now twelve years old and lives at No. 17, Yongnian Lane, Baike Road. In 1934, Shi came to Shanghai from Hankou to visit friends and stayed in Room 49 of the Old Oriental Hotel. Fang Jiaheng, a wealthy young local man, also had a long-term room in Room 83 of the hotel. He found Shi attractive and pursued her, using all kinds of methods to propose to her, saying that his position as the spouse was still open and he wished to stay together until their hair turned white. Shi had just arrived in Shanghai, her resolve was weak, and she agreed to his request. So, they rented a house at No. 13, Zunde Lane, Xiamen Road, and lived together. Shi repeatedly urged him to marry her, but Fang always prevaricated. Later, he gradually became indifferent to Shi, and then stopped coming to her place altogether, abandoning her. After Shi investigated, she learned that Fang was already married. Realizing that she had been deceived, Shi hired a lawyer to sue Fang for abandonment in the First Special District Court. However, Fang consistently failed to appear in court. Later, because the claim did not meet the legal requirements, she lost the case. Now, Shi has hired a lawyer again to file a lawsuit against Fang in the civil division of the First Special District Court, requesting a judgment ordering Fang to pay 3,992 yuan in compensation. Because she was unable to pay the court fees, she applied for legal aid. This morning, Judge Tao Dejun opened the Fourth Civil Chamber for questioning. Fang Jiaheng did not appear and had no lawyer representing him. Shi explained what happened. Because Fang was not present, the proceedings could not continue, and the court adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Rickshaw Puller Pushes Child, Causing Injury and Death from Being Run Over: Corpse Inspected Yesterday

Han Yonglai, a native of Shaoxing who runs a scale shop at No. 477, Dong Ao Bili Road, had a son named Hexian, who was only six years old. At approximately 6:00 PM on the 30th of last month, while Hexian was playing on the sidewalk in front of the shop, a rickshaw No. 1088 came from the west. Three people were pulling the rickshaw in front, and one person was steering it in the back. Wang Qingrong, a 46-year-old man from Jiangbei who was pulling the rickshaw on the left side, was not walking on the road, but on the sidewalk. When he reached that spot, he shouted and, seeing that the child had not left, pushed the child, causing him to lose his balance and fall to the bottom of the sidewalk, where his right leg was run over by the rickshaw wheel. After people saw it, they reported it to the police, who quickly sent the child to Shanghai Sanatorium and Hospital. The treatment was ineffective, and he died at 4:00 PM on the 31st. The police station in charge of the area ordered detectives to investigate and transferred the body to the Philand Road Examination Office. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Tang, appointed by the First Special District District Court, arrived at the office to examine the body. After determining the body, he questioned the witness Dong Fanghao and others about what they had seen. Wang Qingrong was questioned, his statement was evasive, and he denied pulling the rickshaw on the sidewalk. The child's father, Han Yonglai, said that he also witnessed his son being injured and requested redress. Prosecutor Tang obtained the statements and then questioned the Western Police Chief Fu Si, asking if the police station had any opinions on the case. The police chief said that the police station believed that the rickshaw puller was not at fault, so no charges were filed. Prosecutor Tang then concluded that the deceased boy, Han Hexian, had died from being run over by rickshaw No. 1088 while still alive. The body was handed over to his father, Han Yonglai, who signed a guarantee to claim it for burial.

Dai Changrui Sues Tang Yongxin: Hearing Rescheduled for Next Monday

Wu Jusheng, a woman from Suzhou, also known as Tang Wu, is 21 years old. Two years ago, she was married to Tang Yongxin (33 years old), the son of Tang Jinrong, the owner of the Zhenxing Frame Shop at No. 184, Yuyuan Road, Chenghuang Temple, Shanghai, through a matchmaker. After the marriage, the woman discovered that Tang had a venereal disease and was having an affair, which caused marital discord. Recently, she sued Tang for injury in the Shanghai District Court, demanding a divorce, but the case was dismissed on the 26th of last month. Because of the lawsuit, Wu temporarily resided in the home of a relative at No. 9, Lixian Lane, Zilaihu Street, French Concession. On the 11th of last month, Tang Yongxin suddenly gathered a group of people and went to No. 9, Lixian Lane, where he beat Wu and injured her. She reported the incident to the French police, who arrested Tang and took him to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. The hearing continued on the 29th of last month, and Tang Yongxin was found guilty of assault and fined ten yuan. Now, Dai Changrui, a resident of Suzhou and the second landlord of No. 9, Lixian Lane (a clerk at the Wu Bao Law Firm), has filed a complaint in the criminal division of the Second Special District Court, accusing Tang Yongxin of assault, illegal entry into a residence, and property damage, and has filed a civil suit seeking compensation for damages. After reviewing the complaint, the court summoned them to the Second Criminal Chamber yesterday morning with Judge Qiu Huanhu presiding. According to the plaintiff Dai Changrui, on the night of August 11, the defendant's wife, Tang Wu, came to my house to use the phone to inquire about the lawsuit in the district court with her attorney. While they were talking, the defendant arrived with a group of people, first beating Tang Wu and then smashing the objects in my house. My brother heard the noise upstairs and came downstairs, and was also beaten and slightly injured. The defendant and the others then fled. I request an investigation and an order for compensation for the losses. The defendant Tang Yongxin testified that on the night of August 11, I saw my wife and the plaintiff enter No. 9, Lixian Lane, hand in hand. I followed them in and was immediately beaten and fled. Later, he (referring to the plaintiff) called his daughter and brother to beat me. I have bloody clothes and a singlet as evidence. I did not smash anything in his house. The judge asked the plaintiff if he was present when the fight occurred. Dai replied that he was not. The defendant's defense attorney, Mao Xianshen, said that the judge's question about whether the plaintiff was present clearly showed that the plaintiff had fabricated the facts. The defendant has now filed a counterclaim. The court, after reviewing the evidence, stated that the case required the review of the public prosecution file and announced that the hearing would be rescheduled for next Monday.

Pan Gongzhan of the Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association Hosted Captains of Solicitation Teams Yesterday; More Than One Hundred People Including Yu Qiaqing and Wang Xiaolai Attended; Solicitation Period Starts on September 5th for One Month

The Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association of this city, in order to expand the solicitation of members, resolved through the Executive Committee to appoint Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and others as captains of the solicitation teams. Yesterday, the general captain of the association, Pan Gongzhan, specially hosted representatives from all walks of life, various team captains, and the press at the Bankers' Association. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

In addition to Pan Gongzhan, attendees included Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Cai Jingjun, Zhang Huikang, Pan Dechun, Li Dachao, Wu Yun, Chu Jiang Zongyi, Zhang Wenkui, Gu Zhian, Dai Gengxin, Fang Yexian, Guo Shun, Lao Jingxiu, Yang Weiyin, Xue Fuji, Qu Shao Yi, Zhang Lixing, Hu Guigeng, Nie Shiqi, Xiang Shengwu, Lin Kanghou, Wang Jiean, Wang Jingshan, Shao Daru, Pan Yangxiao, Xu Chao, Ren Shigang, Cai Shengbai, Tong Boying, Hu Xiyuan, Yu Tinghui, Guan Jiu'an, Jiang Xiang Qing, Cheng Nianpeng, Zhang Qingfa, Chen Yiting, Fang Jiange, Xu Yunhui, Xu Jianruo, Sun Daosheng, Zheng Hairuo, Chen Jiqing, and more than one hundred others.

Chairman's Report

During the meeting, Chairman Pan Gongzhan reported, "Distinguished guests, today I, representing the Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association, have invited everyone here, hoping that you can assist in our efforts. The Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association was established in the ninth year of the Republic of China and has been in existence for over sixteen years. During the May Fourth period, various circles in Shanghai assisted students in Beiping and achieved considerable goals. At that time, the citizens of Shanghai felt that without a lasting and practical organization, it would be impossible to increase national welfare. Industrial and commercial leaders all felt that to make the country prosperous and strong, it was necessary to promote industry first. Therefore, they initiated the Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association. All citizens should join, as promoting national goods is a great duty that the people should fulfill. In the past, thanks to everyone's efforts, considerable results have been achieved. This time, we are launching an expanded solicitation, hoping that everyone can work hard to ensure its success. As the director of the Social Affairs Bureau, I feel even more duty-bound. Now I am also appointed as a team captain. Overestimating my abilities, I am willing to work together with you all."

Successive Speeches

Next, Sun Daosheng reported on the solicitation methods. The opening ceremony will be held at Zheng Yi She on September 5th, and the closing ceremony will be held on October 5th, with announcements in three phases. Then, Yu Qiaqing said, "I was also one of the initiators of the Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association in the past. In the past, people had a deep-rooted concept of favoring imported goods, making it difficult for domestic goods to develop. Now, with the expansion of solicitation, I hope we can pay attention to counterfeit goods that pass off as national goods, so that the national goods industry can develop. The government should also use legal tender to assist industry and engage in production." Wang Xiaolai then spoke, saying that in times of national crisis, it is necessary to treat the symptoms urgently. The current urgent problems are (1) overpopulation, (2) smuggling, (3) economic issues, and (4) unemployment. These four current difficulties cannot be solved without promoting national goods. Subsequently, Lin Kanghou spoke, stating that in promoting national goods, we should not only pay attention to domestic and international situations but also pay attention to overseas situations and develop overseas shipping routes. Finally, Cai Jingjun, Guan Jiu'an, Hu Xiyuan, and others delivered speeches. The meeting ended in joy at 10 o'clock.

Association Declaration

Our association was established in the ninth year of the Republic of China as the only group for the domestic goods production and consumption sectors to resist foreign economic aggression. Its mission is to arouse the enthusiasm of all citizens in the city to love and use domestic goods and to promote the rational progress of domestic goods factory production. For sixteen years, we have been calling and advocating, never daring to forget this purpose. The people of the country have gained a deep understanding of domestic goods, and domestic goods factories have been able to move forward. Our association has made some contribution, however small it may be. But when examining the customs statistics of the past seventy years, the cumulative trade deficit has reached a huge amount of 1.2 million yuan. Even in the third year of the Republic of China alone, the trade deficit reached 500.03 million yuan. The majority of this huge trade deficit is consumed by urban citizens. It can be asserted that the national goods loving psychology of the people of the country needs to be aroused urgently, and the domestic goods factories need to be supported urgently, and our work needs to be redoubled urgently. This is indeed a matter of urgency. Now, at the beginning of the third solicitation conference of our association, we welcome national goods factory groups to participate in cooperation, and especially welcome individuals to enthusiastically join. Whether you are in agriculture, industry, commerce, study, military, or government, all who consider themselves to have enthusiasm for promoting domestic goods are welcome to join us, to promote universally with the spirit of self-reliance and helping others, to expand the solicitation with the principle of self-awareness and awakening others, to guide each other, and to supervise each other. We must make every citizen of Shanghai a soldier on the front line of national goods, and every factory a rear base for domestic goods. Then the mission of our association can be considered complete.

Organizational Outline

(Organization) The association will have honorary members, 10 to 15 honorary deputy general captains, 1 general captain, 4 deputy general captains, 7 chief staff officers, 30 to 40 team captains. Each team is freely organized by the team captain. (Objective) The total objective is 6,000 shares (1 yuan per share). The minimum objective for each team is 200 shares. (Membership) Divided into factory members, business members, individual members, and special members. (Membership Fee) Factory and business members are divided into three categories: 200 yuan, 100 yuan, and 50 yuan. Individual members are divided into three categories: 100 yuan, 10 yuan, and 1 yuan. Special members are technical talents who sincerely support the association's cause or have made special contributions and products, who can be admitted to the association free of charge upon approval by the executive committee. (Rights) Members of the association have the right to enjoy product certification, apply for rewards, exempt miscellaneous taxes, participate in national exhibitions, provide relief to those wrongly accused, protect interests, mediate disputes, resolve difficulties, design publicity, introduce sales, and speak, propose, vote, elect, and be elected.

List of Team Captains

Honorary General Captain: Wu Tiecheng. Honorary Deputy General Captains: Wang Xiaowei, Du Yuesheng, Wu Kaixian, Lin Kanghou, Yu Zuoting, Yuan Ludeng, Lao Jingxiu, Yu Hede, Cai Jingjun, Dai Gengxin, Wei Tingrong, Yang Xiaotian. General Captain: Pan Gongzhan. Deputy General Captains: Wu Yunchu, Shao Daru, Hu Xiyuan, Cai Shengbai. Chief Staff Officers: Wang Xingyao, Wang Jiean, Li Dachao, Sun Daosheng, Pan Yangyao, Xue Dubi, Chen Yiting. Team Captains: Fang Yexian, Fang Jiange, Ren Shigang, Zai Jingshan, Jin Youcheng, Mi Jifang, Hu Guigeng, Shi Yucun, Yao Defu, Hong Xiaoxian, Yuan Hesong, Xu Yefu, Xu Xiaochu, Chen Yiting, Chen Jiqing, Chen Guangzong, Zhang Zuan, Zhang Wenwei, Zhang Huikang, Zhang Qingfa, Guo Shun, Xiang Kangyuan, Ye Youcai, Xue Fuji, Gu Quansheng, Li Dachao, Xu Guan Qun, Yang Weiyin, Chen Shengju, Zheng Hairuo, Xiang Longxun, Ye Fukan, Zhang Lixing, Qian Jihua. Unpleasant Weather, Continuing River Tides; Major Tides Expected from the 12th; Many Suffering from Dysentery

The early autumn weather in this port is quite sultry and feels unpleasant. There are many overcast days. This morning, there was also drifting rain. The high tide of the Huangpu River continues. Our reporter has filed the following reports:

Unfavorable Climate

The early autumn weather in this port is especially hot. The midday temperature rises to a high degree, only recently turning cooler. The market is full of autumn scenery, but the weather is unpleasant. There are many cloudy days. This morning, there was also rainfall. Residents are losing their adjustment to the climate, leading to a severe epidemic of dysentery.

Continuing New Tides

According to the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau, the Huangpu River will experience continued high tides starting on the morning of the 2nd. The measured times and quantities are as follows: 0:40 AM on the 2nd, high tide quantity was 11 feet 4.5 inches; 1:15 AM on the 3rd, high tide quantity was 11 feet 6.5 inches; 1:53 AM on the 4th, high tide quantity was 10 feet 4.5 inches. It will gradually decrease from the 4th. However, high tides are predicted again from the 12th, with quantities higher than the recent high tides.

He confessed that Qi Ronggui, a native of Anhui residing at No. 8, Lane 366, Dengtu Road, Public Concession, was involved. The day before yesterday, Detective Gu reported to the Huishan Police Station, requesting assistance in the arrest. Chief Constable Wang Shuchen dispatched detectives to secretly go to the address at 11:45 PM, arrested Qi, and searched for counterfeit money without success. Sixty-two Mauser bullets were found in a cloth bag under his bed. All were taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Municipal Council, explained the situation, stating that the defendant denied the counterfeit money case at the police station, claiming that the bullets were collected when selling old goods in Zhabei. He requested an extension for temporary detention, pending transfer by the Public Security Bureau. Detective Wang then reported the incident. The bullets were presented as evidence. When questioned, Qi Ronggui stated that he did not know Chen Longde. He bought a total of 220 bullets. The remaining lead medicine was removed from the copper shell and sold to a copper shop. Regarding the counterfeit banknote incident, a friend named Lao Wu mentioned to him that a certain foreigner wanted him to sell them on commission, and asked "Can you take this on?", to which he refused. The rest of his confession was evasive. Judge Xiao Xiecai ruled that he would remain in custody and the case would be rescheduled for review.

French Concession Clothes Vendors: Two Prohibited Rules Stipulated

The Shanghai French Concession Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the Clothing Industry Association yesterday, stating: "Dear Sirs, We have received your letter of August 11th, stating that the French Police have been abusing their power by fining clothing vendors who set up stalls and shout to sell their wares, and requesting us to negotiate. Our association has repeatedly sent personnel to negotiate, and only yesterday did we meet with the chief of the police station. The chief orally proposed two prohibited rules and asked us to inform all clothing vendors to abide by them: (1) Clothes must be hung at least 0.25 meters (equivalent to 2 ma 1 quad) off the ground, which is 7 Chi in the Shanghai scale; (2) The base of the stall must not obstruct pedestrian traffic by more than 0.08 meters (equivalent to slightly less than 2 and a half Chi in the Shanghai scale). If the above three rules are not violated, there will be no more fines in the future. We have received the letter and are now forwarding the information accordingly. Please investigate and inform everyone concerned."

Poland Restricts Importing Goods via Postal Mail

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 1347 states: "We have received a letter from the Polish Postal Administration stating that for all goods listed in the Polish import declaration, except for those accompanied by a permit issued by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry of this country, they may not be imported by mail. However, the following items do not need to be accompanied by the permit: (1) Foreign language periodicals with illustrations; (2) Foreign language periodicals and foreign language newspapers without illustrations; (3) Polish language periodicals with illustrations, permitted by the Polish Ministry of Finance; (4) Polish language periodicals and Polish language newspapers without illustrations, whose editorial office is located outside the Polish customs territory; (5) Loose photographs (even if made in the style of postal postcards) and photographs sent to newspaper or periodical offices as writing and editing materials; (6) Blueprints or drawings of machines and equipment imported by local machine and equipment manufacturers; (7) Books and pamphlets such as advertising price lists and descriptions of foreign companies, or tourist guides and promotions about foreign tourists; (8) Loose cardboard models made for advertising and explanatory purposes; (9) Labels, books, and stamps for Polish products, sent by foreign buyers to the manufacturers of the products, and having completed customs procedures; (10) Old clothes, old shirts, and old leather shoes donated by foreigners to poor Polish people, with certificates issued by the Polish consulate allowing duty-free delivery. We are forwarding this information for your attention. This notice is issued by Director Zha Peilin, August 29th."

Robbing Police Equipment and Shooting Police Officer: Lin Weixue Blew Police Whistle Frantically and Died After Being Shot

Lin Weixue, a 21-year-old policeman from Suzhou in the Public Security Bureau's Caojiadu branch in Huxi, this city, was assigned to serve at the station by the main bureau, and had not yet been there for two months. At around 8 PM last night, he was on duty at the No. 2 post in front of the dormitory of the Central Geological Research Institute on Jessfield Road. Suddenly, two armed bandits, taking advantage of the dim night, rushed forward and robbed Lin of his pistol. The policeman resisted with all his might, while frantically blowing his police whistle to call for help, and tried to draw his gun to defend himself. Fearing being captured, the robbers shot at Lin. One bullet hit the policeman's right leg, penetrating his bladder. He immediately collapsed to the ground in a pool of blood, unconscious with pain. The robbers, seeing what they had done, fled in haste and disappeared without a trace. Nearby police officers heard the whistle and came to the scene, finding Policeman Lin lying injured in a pool of blood. They immediately ran back to the branch to report. The branch chief, Tan Baochou, upon hearing the news, went to the scene himself and sent the injured policeman to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road for treatment. Due to excessive blood loss, he died at around 1 AM this morning. The bureau reported the incident to the main bureau, requesting compensation, and ordered the detective squad of the branch to track down the fleeing criminals and bring them to justice to warn future offenders. It is said that Policeman Lin has an elderly father of over 60 years old living in his hometown. A telegram has been sent to notify him to come to Shanghai to take care of the aftermath.

Peanut Harvest Abundant, Indian Production Reduced

Shen Shi News Agency reports that peanuts are an important agricultural product of our country and a major export commodity. They are produced in all provinces, including Jiangsu, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Sichuan, Hunan, Yunnan, Fujian, Guangdong, Jiangxi, Shandong, Shanxi, Shaanxi, and Hebei. The largest cultivation areas are in Hebei, Henan, and Shandong provinces. In addition to supplying domestic consumption, peanuts are also exported overseas. Since the 15th year of the Republic of China, the export of peanuts from our country has gradually increased, reaching its peak in the 20th year of the Republic of China, with annual exports reaching over 18 million yuan, ranking tenth among export commodities. This year, the peanut production in our country is very abundant, increasing by one-third compared to last year, while the peanut production in India is not abundant. Therefore, the export of peanuts from our country is expected to improve this year. India is a major supplier in the world peanut market, so the export of peanuts from our country depends on the abundance of the peanut harvest in India.

Detailed Record of Zhu Atao's Wife-Killing Case: A Major Tragedy Resulting from Minor Disputes; The Murderer Confesses to Being Mentally Unstable

First, Attorney Zhang Tianyin of the police station filed a public prosecution against the defendant Zhu Atao in accordance with Article 271 of the Criminal Law regarding the crime of murder, and detailed

The Circumstances of the Case

He stated that the defendant, Zhu Atao, is from Pudong, 26 years old, and has been engaged in setting up mutton stalls. Last year, on the fifth day of the twelfth lunar month, he married Yang Fengxian, a 19-year-old Ningbo woman, through a matchmaker. They lived together at No. 9 Taian Lane, Tian'an Road, while Zhu worked at the Xinglong Noodle Shop at No. 633 Tian'an Road nearby, but it was on a voluntary basis without pay, which caused him to feel quite poor. As a result, he often quarreled with his wife, Yang, and their relationship deteriorated day by day. On the 30th of last month, at about 1:00 PM, the defendant, because it was his wife's brother's son's

One-Month Celebration

Went to his wife's brother Yang Arong's house at No. 27 Yuelaifang, Tiantong Road, to drink. He noticed that his wife's clothes were dirty, her shoes were broken, and she had no socks, so he advised her to go home and tidy up her clothes to avoid being indecent. After speaking, Zhu also went out to work in the shop. Unexpectedly, in the evening, Zhu saw his wife walking on the road, still in the same state, and started an argument. At that time, Zhu was slapped twice by his wife. He immediately went home, took the clothes out of the box and pawned them, bought opium with the money, intending to commit suicide, and also

Completely Destroyed

All the belongings in the house without saying goodbye. Zhu was helpless at the time. After thinking about it, he became angrier. So, at 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, he secretly hid a mutton knife and went out to find his wife, intending to kill her. Unexpectedly, when he passed the noodle shop at No. 633 Tiantong Road, he suddenly saw his wife walking out of the noodle shop. Without asking why, he pulled out the sharp blade and slashed Zhu Yang's back and buttocks twice, causing her to fall to the ground. But Zhu was still not satisfied and continued to slash her in the thighs and lower abdomen, causing her to bleed all over the ground. The knife wounds were very severe, and she fell into a coma,

Unconscious

Her brother, Yang Arong, called Chinese Constable No. 1604 to arrest Zhu and sent her by car to the Shanghai Sanitarium on Laobazi Road, but the treatment was ineffective, and she died shortly afterward. The body is now awaiting examination at the coroner's office. However, the police station examined the reason for the defendant's wife-killing this time, fearing that there might be other motives, and asked for an interrogation. The defendant, Zhu Atao, confessed, "Since I married Yang, our relationship has been bad. The other day, for my wife's brother's son's full moon, the deceased wore broken shoes with no socks and dirty clothes. I forbade her to go out, but she would not listen and started arguing with me, tearing my

Clothes

And buying opium to threaten suicide, and expressing her unwillingness to be a wife to a poor man like me, and wishing to marry a rascal. At that time, I ordered her to return to Pudong, but she refused. Therefore, a big quarrel broke out, and the deceased also went out in anger. Yesterday afternoon, I

Hid a Mutton Knife

Searching for my wife, I saw her coming out of the noodle shop, so I slashed her right leg and back twice. After she fell to the ground, I slashed her three more times, but I don't know where the last three slashes landed because my mind was already unclear," etc. Judge Huang instructed that the case be adjourned for seven days for further questioning, and the defendant was remanded in custody. The Death of the Famous Painter Zhang Xian

Zhang Xian, professor of Western painting at the Shanghai Art College, was a native of Qingtian, Zhejiang. As a child, he was gifted and fond of art. In 1922, he graduated from the college and then served in the education circles of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. However, he never fulfilled his wish. In 1931, he went to France and studied at the Paris School of Fine Arts. Due to a lack of funds, he worked in a factory at night to support himself through diligent work and study. In four years, he achieved a deep understanding of oil painting and sketching. The great painter Aenaes Laurent called him his top student. In 1927, he returned to China and became a professor at his alma mater. In 1929, his teacher Liu Haisu went to Europe and accompanied him to the Fa Yijia study session. He extensively viewed famous works of ancient and modern times and was influenced by other literary, artistic, political, and educational figures. His life drawing and freehand drawing both reached a state of divine skill, making him a prominent master. In November 1931, he returned to China and resumed his position as a Western painting professor at the art college, tirelessly teaching and guiding future generations. Hundreds of his students admired and respected him. In his spare time, he often painted himself, devoting his life to art without seeking fame or recognition. His colleagues in the art world also competed to praise him. In recent years, he attacked white-line drawing figures in Chinese painting. The lines were dynamic and swirling, purely natural and not artificial. Although it seemed simple, it contained an elusive sense of strength. Those who knew said that Zhang's white-line drawing ladies had the beauty of Jia Long (Li Longmian) and Yu Yu (Ding Nanyu), opening an era in the Chinese art world. He also used the charm of Chinese painting in oil painting, integrating Eastern elements with the Greek tradition, expressing a calm tone and smooth lines, solving the secrets of art. He was truly an outstanding figure among Chinese painters. Unfortunately, he suddenly contracted liver disease during his summer vacation and was mistakenly treated with medicine, leading to his death in his hometown on the 14th of this month. He was only 38 years old. His death was desolate, and friends and relatives were shocked and saddened when they heard the news. Zhang's ambition died with him, and heaven did not grant him a long life. It is truly a great loss to the art world. The only consolation is that he left behind a forest of works, all of which are successful works. Liu Haisu and others plan to launch an orphan education committee for Zhang's orphans, hold a posthumous exhibition of his works on a regular basis, raise education funds for the orphans, and publish a collection of his posthumous works to commemorate him and take good care of his affairs. All students and colleagues at the art college decided to hold a memorial service after the start of school.

Xie Hengchuang Case Settled

Xie Hengchuang, a Ningbo native, coal magnate of Yuchang Coal Company (above the Shanghai Women's Bank building on Nanjing Road) and chairman of the Coal Industry Association, was recently sued by Tong Weibin, owner of Yichangtai Construction Factory, in the Civil Court of the Second Special Court for failing to repay a deposit of 16,612 yuan, 2 jiao, and 5 fen in principal and interest. According to the plaintiff's complaint, the plaintiff contracted to build all the Kang Le Cun housing at the intersection of Fuxu Road and Moore Road in 1933, and the defendant later owed 15,496 yuan in construction costs. Because the defendant was unable to pay, the debt was converted into a deposit at the defendant's Yuchang Coal Company after mediation, stipulating a weekly interest rate of 6%. By December 5, 1934, the total debt was 16,612 yuan, 2 jiao, and 5 fen. Because the defendant repeatedly delayed payment, a lawsuit was filed. The court accepted the complaint and Judge Li Liang opened a court session to summon the defendant, Xie Hengchuang. Because Xie Hengchuang was avoiding the summer heat in Lushan, he was unable to attend and only委托 a lawyer to appear in court and request a postponement. Details have been recorded in this newspaper. It is now known that the two parties have reached a settlement out of court during the postponement. Yesterday morning, Judge Li opened a court session to continue the hearing. Both parties were represented by lawyers who presented the settlement terms. The defendant Xie Hengchuang will pay off all the debt within three months, and the defendant will bear the litigation costs. The lawyers for both parties then signed the settlement record in court and left the court.

Ministry of Finance's Approval of Doubts About Stamping Duplicate Invoices

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to inquire whether duplicate invoices should be stamped. Yesterday, it received Approval No. 税字 (tax character) 10552 from the Ministry of Finance: "Your telegram is noted. According to the provisions of Article 3, Paragraph 7 of the Stamp Tax Law, if the original of various certificates has been affixed with stamp tax票, the duplicate should be exempt from stamping. According to the provisions of Article 7 of the same law, when the duplicate is used as the original, it should still be affixed with stamps. Therefore, whether the duplicate should be stamped depends on whether it is used. A delivery invoice is a certificate issued with the goods and given to the customer. The duplicate invoice used by the Huade 工廠 (factory), if it is given to the collector to take to the other party for inspection and is not left in the hands of the other party, cannot be considered as used as the original and can be exempt from stamping. If it is given to the customer, it is used as the original and should still be stamped according to law. You should immediately instruct them to comply with this approval."

Central Bank Inspection Report

This cash reserve includes 10,813,8205.9 yuan stored in the bank's issuing head office and branch warehouses and branches, 9,649,9069.71 yuan deposited with other banks, and 10,131,8100 yuan in guaranteed reserves converted into silver. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange certificates issued is 400,9630.07 yuan, with a reserve including 7926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68 customs gold, totaling 400,9630.07 yuan. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, cash reserves must be at least 60 percent, and the remainder must be guaranteed by legal collateral. The inspection results show that the cash reserves exceed 60 percent, and the guaranteed reserves are within 40 percent, which is in accordance with the law. This is a special report. August 31, 1936, Li Fuxun, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiyu."

Death of Doctor Pan Yuanruo

Doctor Pan Yuanruo of the Shanghai Municipal Hospital unfortunately suffered from scarlet fever complicated by pneumonia and died on August 29. Pan, with the courtesy name Yuanruo, was a native of Suzhou. He graduated from Tongji University and served as an attending physician in internal medicine at Baolong Hospital. He was currently the chief physician in internal medicine at the Shanghai Municipal Hospital. He was knowledgeable and experienced. It is reported that he was married for only four months when he suddenly passed away, and colleagues in the medical profession deeply mourned his loss and will hold a memorial service soon.

Hu Xiyuan's Radio Speech: A Simple Explanation of Promoting National Products

I have never been good at giving speeches, but today it is my turn to give a speech. Isn't this a difficult thing? Moreover, everyone is very familiar with the term "promoting national products." However, the topic of my speech today is still these four words. Ladies and gentlemen, think about how broad and familiar this is. Mr. Cai Shengbai, Mr. Pan Yangyao, and many other people who are enthusiastic about national products have already explained it very thoroughly. What else can I say? Isn't this a difficult problem?

Speaking of promoting national products, it is the duty of every citizen, and it is the natural duty of every citizen. This sentence is not to plagiarize other people's old tunes. I think the promotion of national products is something that the public should generally know. There is no need to cite profound theories. I will talk about some simple metaphors that can be understood.

For example, there is a Li Family Village with dozens of households and hundreds of acres of farmland. They are very self-sufficient and do not need to rely on the help of other villages. However, although the Li Family Village has a very good harvest every year, they do not have a rice milling machine. Therefore, the rice they produce every year is either used to pay for milling fees and they ask the neighboring Zhang Family Village to mill the rice, or they first sell the grain to the Zhang Family Village at a very low price, and then buy rice from the Zhang Family Village at a high price to make a living. In this way, although the Li Family Village has a good harvest every year, all its profits are exploited by the Zhang Family Village. Ladies and gentlemen, think about it, if this continues, won't the Li Family Village be poor every day?

Later, a certain Jia in the Li Family Village came up with the idea to buy several rice milling machines, and he milled the grain for the villagers at a very low price to avoid giving all the colorful and green legal tender to the Zhang Family Village. Who knew that most of the people in the Li Family Village were ignorant? Although a certain Jia bought several machines, they did not trust him and still sold the grain cheaply and bought rice back at a high price. Wouldn't this make a certain Jia feel greatly disappointed and discouraged?

In my metaphor, the Li Family Village is our Republic of China, the Zhang Family Village is a foreign country, that is, the great powers, and a certain Jia is of course a domestic factory.

There is another metaphor about human nature. Domestic products are like our own children, and foreign products are like other people's children. We should love, guide, and hope for the development of our own children's careers. This is certain. Would we be willing to love other people's children who have nothing to do with us and turn a blind eye to our own lovely children who are displaced? I think anyone with a human heart would never do this.

The purpose of establishing domestic factories is not entirely for profit, but to recover the money flowing out and preserve the country's financial resources. This is self-evident. All citizens of the Republic of China should support and protect them. How can they ignore the survival of domestic factories and the many employees and workers who rely on making a living, and send precious money to foreign countries?

In the past, our industry was not developed, and almost all the necessities of clothing, food, housing, and transportation were not produced in our country. Even some handmade goods were no longer suitable for practical use due to the evolution of the times. Therefore, we had to seek them from foreign countries. Now, what kind of industry is there that we do not have domestic products? Moreover, some domestic products are cheap and of good quality. Then, to use foreign products again, isn't that crazy?

People who have studied abroad seem to like to use foreign goods. However, I am not saying that all students who have studied abroad do not like to use domestic products. However, there is indeed a part of people who have been gilded abroad who worship foreign goods the most and want to turn their faces into blue eyes and blond hair. Well, speaking of these people, they are all outstanding members of the Republic of China and have profound knowledge. Wouldn't you feel sad when you think about such ingratitude?

According to a survey by the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, the value of foreign imported goods in our country in 1934 exceeded the value of exported domestic products by 494,450,945 yuan in national currency. In 1935, it exceeded 144,340,262 yuan. Just in the first half of this year, it will exceed 126,288,775 yuan. Ladies and gentlemen, our country is now economically exhausted to the extreme. If this continues, I am afraid that those who are now called the rich will become poor, and the current poor will become starving corpses. At that time, even if other countries do not use force to invade, we will have already perished due to economic collapse. This is such a dangerous and terrible thing. We might as well not talk about promoting domestic products. Otherwise, we must practice it ourselves. We must treat the promotion of domestic products like a religion. From now on, except for necessities that are not available in our country, we swear not to buy any foreign goods. We must always have the desire to preserve the country's financial resources. Only then will our Republic of China have the hope of revival.

Now it's time. When I have the opportunity, I will talk to you again next time. Goodbye.

Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Changes Report for the Second Quarter of This Year (Continued) (Thirty-Fifth Overview of Shanghai Industry and Commerce)

— Edited by China Credit

A. Important Industrial and Commercial Changes in April

A. Financial Industry:

1. Opening of the Shanghai Branch of the Sichuan Salt Bank: The head office of the bank is located in Chongqing. In addition to Shanghai, the branch also has two locations in Chengdu and Zigong, and offices in Luxian and Jiangjin. The total capital is 2 million national currency. Recently, in order to develop its business, it has newly established a branch in Shanghai, which was announced to be open on the 14th.

2. Suspension of Business of the British and American China Bank: The bank was established on January 15 of this year in cooperation with the Da Xin Industrial Bank. Initially, it was a Sino-American joint venture. Later, due to the withdrawal of American shares, British and overseas Chinese joined, so it was called a British company. It was registered with the Hong Kong government with a fixed capital of 1 million yuan, but the actual paid-up amount was said to be less than half. The official opening ceremony was just held on the 8th of this month, and on the 30th, it suddenly announced a financial crunch due to a small amount of more than 4,000 yuan, which forced it to suspend business temporarily.

3. Liquidation of Yicheng Qianzhuang: The firm, also known as Yicheng Qianzhuang, just opened in March. The owner is Mr. Qiu Zuxian, with a capital of only a few thousand yuan. After operating until now, less than a month, it announced that it could not maintain. It is almost a special phenomenon in the economic downturn of the market that it closed down one after another with the America China Bank.

B. Industrial Sector:

1. Establishment of Xinfeng Weaving and Printing Silk Cloth Factory: The factory was originally a partnership. Recently, in order to expand its business, the original shareholders decided to add new shares and reorganize into a limited liability company. The capital amount was set at 200,000 yuan, and the full amount has been raised. A founding meeting was held on the 24th, and Mr. Shen Liucun was elected as the chairman and manager.

2. Establishment of Zhongming Machinery Company: The company specializes in manufacturing Zhongming-style wood-charcoal car oil substitute stoves. The factory is located at No. 270 Qiqihar Road. It was officially announced on the 1st of this month. The chairman is Mr. Fan Zhengbo, and the manager is Mr. Tang Yunqing.

3. Reopening of Changming Electrical Appliance Company: The factory initially specialized in manufacturing flashlights and other items. Later, due to fierce competition in the same industry, the managers realized that it was unprofitable, so they specialized in making clocks, which achieved good results. Unexpectedly, the factory suddenly caught fire in January of this year, and all its essence was destroyed, with losses amounting to 200,000 yuan. This time, the shareholders, in view of the difficulty of starting a business in the past, re-collected a capital of 100,000 yuan, built new factory buildings, and reinstalled machines. It was announced to reopen on the 5th of this month.

4. Qingli Zhao Pan of Zhonghua Fengji Glass Factory: The factory originally belonged to a Japanese company. Later, due to operating losses, it was transferred to Mr. Cao Fengbiao, a Chinese businessman, for operation. The business was still considerable. Unexpectedly, the "January 28th" incident broke out. The factory was located on the front line and was completely destroyed by artillery fire. Although Mr. Cao struggled to reopen after the war, the economic downturn enveloped everywhere, and the factory eventually announced Qingli Zhao Pan due to sluggish business.

5. Liquidation of Diantong Company: The company appeared in the film industry in 1934 with a brand-new appearance. The paid-up capital was 100,000 yuan. The general manager was Mr. Ma Jiande. The business was originally said to be good. Recently, due to the harsh environment, it had no intention of operating, so it was officially announced for liquidation on the 30th of this month.

C. Commercial Sector:

1. Opening of Daxing Transportation and Sales Trading Company: The company was initiated by giant merchants such as Du Yuesheng and Lu Bohong, specializing in the transportation and sales of domestic Guangdong local sugar and agricultural products such as beans and wheat in the Yangtze River Basin. The chairman is Mr. Du Yuesheng, and the general manager is Mr. Zheng Zenan. Transactions will start on the 26th of this month, and the opening will be held regularly.

2. Opening of Shanghai Fish Market: The market has been planned and built by the Ministry of Industry for a long time. Initially, it was planned to be completely state-owned. Later, in order to take into account the interests of the fish merchants, the Ministry of Industry changed it to a joint venture between officials and merchants. The fixed capital is 1.2 million national currency, which is a joint-stock company. The general manager is Mr. Wang Xiaolai. The market can open a new era for the transportation and sales of China's fishery in the future.

3. Opening of Shanghai Fuxing National Products Company: The company inherited the original business of the former Shanghai National Products Company. Mr. Chen Zhong and others formed the preparatory committee of Shanghai Fuxing National Products Co., Ltd., and revitalized the business on the original foundation. Transactions started on the 1st of this month.

4. Opening of Shanghai Huayang Grocery Cooperative: The cooperative is composed of 14 companies in the same industry of Huayang grocery stores, including Dafengchang, Tongchang, Yiyuan, Hengxing, Zhendachang, Yuanfeng, Hechangxiang, Xiedachang, Hengchang, Xintaichang, Qingda, Yongtaichang, Juchengchang, and Tongyitai, specializing in obtaining the management rights of the products of various factories and acting as sales agents. (To be continued)

1500 Meter Preliminary Round

(51) Football Match: Zero to Two, We Lost to England

The football tournament adopted an elimination system. In the first battle, our country met the founder of football, the English team. It was really an unfortunate thing. The reporter said in the previous newsletter that our team has gathered the best players in the country, dominating the Far East. For decades, the technology is definitely not inferior to any strong team in the country, but the physical strength is not as good as others. It is estimated that the first half will not show weakness, and the second half will definitely fail. As a result, it turned out to be as expected.

European countries seem to know the strength of our team very well. A newspaper the day before yesterday predicted that in the Sino-British football match, there would be no record in the first half, and the British could win two goals in the second half. It was really guessed correctly. The British team did not dare to underestimate us at all before the war. Their coach was even worried about being eliminated by our country. The British Emperor sent a telegram to encourage their players, telling them to work hard and maintain the honor of national skills. The Sino-British football war is valued, which can be seen from this.

The football tournament stipulates that the semi-finals and finals are held at the conference venue. The venue for the Sino-British football match is called CommsonSpartplatz, which is far from the conference venue, but there are more than 10,000 spectators, which is more than any initial audience. Our government representative Dai Jitao and the ambassador to Germany Cheng Tianfang are both guests in the special seats. Five or six hundred students from European countries, including students in Germany, also formed a cheering squad. Of course, there were also many British expatriates watching the game. Japanese players also all set off to watch the big battle on the sidelines. The speed of the British team's movements was indeed not as good as our team's. The difference in physical strength was very far. However, the shooting skills were not seen to be excellent. Otherwise, we would have lost one or two more goals, which would also be expected. The defensive strength of the Chinese side is much stronger than the forwards. First, the goalkeeper Bao Jiaping is definitely meritorious and innocent. Two or three dangerous balls were saved by him. As for the two goals lost, they were all shot in from a distance of ten to fifteen yards in front of the goal. Even if he had three heads and six arms, there was nothing he could do. Tan Jiangbai and Li Tiansheng were even more hardworking. If it weren't for their copper head and iron shovel, the result of this battle would have been unimaginable. Their old-fashioned skills and heroic ball-saving won a lot of applause from the whole stadium. Even the British reporters sitting next to the reporter praised them a lot. The two goals that were missed, of course, they cannot but bear some responsibility. However, the best defense is offense. The ball is always hovering in our area, how can there not be any loss of learning? The central defenders Xu Yahui and Chen Zhenhe still maintain their inherent skills. The offense and defense are organized and reasonable. Huang Meishun's reckless action made the strong British players a little scared, but he was too reckless and violated many rules, and was punished with many free kicks. As for the forwards, Li Huitang was burdened by his reputation and was closely monitored by the enemy. As soon as the ball reached his feet, two or three people came to grab it, so there were few opportunities to move. This is one of the reasons for the weakness of the offensive power. Feng Jingxiang is lively and agile, full of courage, and can be called quiet as a virgin and moving as a rabbit. Sun Jinshun's head and feet are strong and his movements are old-fashioned, but he is too slow and delays many opportunities. Cao Guicheng and Ye Beihua have no achievements to speak of, especially Ye Beihua, who has almost no good performance. With such wings, it is of course as difficult as climbing to the sky to make achievements. As far as the battle strategy is concerned, our team used short passes entirely. Of course, we must be cautious in the face of strong enemies, but there are too many short passes, which allows the enemy to arrange and defend from the loss of value. Furthermore, the speed of passing the ball is not fast enough, so it is often intercepted by the enemy. However, on the whole, in the 90-minute bloody battle, our risk has fully demonstrated the power of the Far East overlord. Although we lost two goals, we did not feel chilly. Let's cut the crap and get back to the topic. At 5:20 PM, the players from China and England lined up in double rows and walked into the stadium with the ball in the hands of the two captains. The whole stadium applauded warmly. They each took one side and practiced shooting. Ten minutes later, the referee called the captains of the two teams to determine the direction. Li Huitang won the first prize and designated to sit facing south from the north. With a whistle, the two sides opened the following formations:

No gains in the first half

The English team kicked off first to attack. Ye Beihua stepped forward and intercepted it, passing it to Li Huitang. Li led the troops to advance. After two or three passes, he was blocked by the English central defender and handed it to the forward, who pressed forward. Tan Jiangbai calmly saved the situation, turning danger into safety. The English army attacked again, Kyle raised his foot to shoot, Bao Jiaping caught it squarely and kicked it out. It was intercepted by Joey again, and Xu Yahui grabbed the ball anxiously, violating military regulations, and was penalized with a free kick at 40 yards. Xu turned back to protect and made up for his mistakes. The English army's offensive was very strong, and after two or three rounds, they penetrated deep into the hinterland. Crawford raised his foot and shot forcefully, and Tan Jiangbai's copper head was applauded by the audience. After that, our army advanced twice from the right, but both returned without success. When the enemy attacked us, it also took great pains. At six minutes, Tan Jiangbai was guilty of foul play and was penalized with a free kick at 30 yards. Tawz raised his foot and shot fiercely, flying high out of bounds. In the melee until twelve minutes, Li Huitang led the army to counterattack for the third time, pressing into the enemy's formation, but because of the strict defense, he could not penetrate deeply. Cao Guicheng once shot, but it was caught by the enemy goalkeeper. After that, the two sides were in chaos and both came to a dead end. At 32 minutes, the enemy army committed a handball in the middle of the money, and Huitang kicked it out but was intercepted. At 34 minutes, Ye Beihua got the ball and moved forward quickly, all the way to the baseline, and passed it in with one kick. Feng Jingxiang did not hit the head and missed a good opportunity. At 35 minutes, the enemy army took advantage of our empty defense and flew in. Bao Jiaping guarded the empty goal alone, and the situation was critical. Winterson was eager to win and missed slightly out of bounds. It was extremely dangerous for this ball not to be lost. At 37 minutes, Huang Meishun got the ball and passed it far, and Li Huitang took the opportunity to press forward, but the ball was intercepted by Joey and kicked out in one kick, hitting Huitang's abdomen squarely, causing great damage to his vitality. He stopped for half a minute and fortunately recovered. After that, you came and I went, and no one made any achievements. The first half ended, and everyone was empty-handed.

Losing Two Goals, We Were Finally Eliminated

After eating the lemons, we reorganized our troops and fought again. Our team reversed the previous state and adopted an offensive. The central defenders came out to help the battle, and the momentum was very strong. At four minutes, Cao Guicheng got the ball and passed it to Sun Jinshun. Sun passed two levels and passed it back to Cao Guicheng. At this time, the enemy's rear defense was empty, and he could do whatever he wanted, but Cao Guicheng was one step late, and all hope was in vain. The opportunity was given to the enemy cavalry, which became rampant again, with a surging momentum, waving their spears and pressing forward. Fortunately, the copper head and iron shovel resisted with all their might, and the steel gates also showed their skills many times, so they were not ambushed. However, a wise man will make a mistake, and at eleven minutes, the enemy army came back and Tawz sneaked through the difficulty. At ten yards, he greeted the door and swept angrily. Although the steel gate had three heads and six arms, it was difficult to reverse the tide. Although our army lost one goal, the momentum did not weaken slightly. The forward line tried to cheer up the meaning of the handsome instruction, but it was always off by a millimeter, and the error was thousands of times. At 19 minutes, Huan knocked on the enemy gate, and Jinshun unfortunately fouled. Although he fired a cannon to break the town, he could only win the sighs of the fans. Cao Guicheng woke up from his sleep, drew his bow and shot an arrow, but it flew far away and did not hit the key point. Two minutes later, the enemy cavalry came like hungry tigers pouncing on food, arranging to overwhelm the sea. Li Tan could not save it, and Etesden waved his steel legs and fought hard to save it in front of the door, but he was exhausted and lost another city. The general situation was gone, and after that, our army tried to counterattack many times, but the enemy army firmly cleared the fields, how easy it was, and the troops were withdrawn. With a score of 0 to 1, our team was eliminated.

Our National World Games Soccer Team Loses to Corinthians in England; Physical Strength Inferior, Losing 2-3 by One Goal; Led 2-0 in the First Half; English Team Scores Three Consecutive Goals to Turn the Tide

Reuters, London, 31st – The Chinese World Games soccer team played its first match in England today, losing 2-3 to the Corinthians team (Islington Corinthians) due to inferior physical strength. The match was held at Arsenal's Highbury stadium, attracting a large crowd.

In the first half, the Chinese team performed admirably, leading 2-1 with excellent teamwork. The five forwards launched fierce attacks, penetrating the enemy territory. The center-back also adopted an offensive approach, providing support from behind. After the start of the match, the Chinese team quickly took the lead, scoring twice in succession. Within twenty minutes, center forward Feng Jingxiang and left inside Li Huitang each scored a goal. Shortly before the end of the first half, Tonington of Corinthians salvaged a goal.

After switching sides, the English team gradually gained the upper hand with their physical strength. Osborne and Lewis scored one after the other, leaving the Chinese team with no chance to retaliate. Li Huitang, center back Liang Rongzhao, and center half Huang Meishun performed best for the Chinese team.

Qiu Feihai Memorial Tournament This Sunday at the French Club; Matches Scheduled from 2:30 PM, Three Matches Arranged; Tickets at One Yuan, All Proceeds to Benefit Family, Season Tickets and Complimentary Tickets Not Valid

Mr. Qiu Feihai, a famous Chinese tennis player, passed away in Gulangyu last month due to illness. His passing left his family in dire straits, with almost no means of livelihood. Enthusiastic members of the tennis community in this city, such as Chen Qihao, Hu Xiansheng, and Li Baojun, originally planned to hold several charity exhibition matches at the Country Club grounds last Sunday. The proceeds from ticket sales were to be remitted to Mr. Qiu's family for relief. However, due to the sudden rush of time, they planned to postpone the event. Unexpectedly, the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association, organized by Westerners, heard of this and expressed great sympathy. They offered to hold a large-scale competition at their club grounds, which has more seating, with all ticket sales for the day donated to Mr. Qiu's family. Details of this have been previously reported.

Match Order Already Arranged

The order of the matches has been arranged by the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Association. It includes a semi-final of the senior grass court tournament, a final of the Roper Cup doubles, and a special exhibition match. It is scheduled to start at 2:30 PM this Sunday (6th) at the French Club grounds on Route Ghisi, Avenue Mesny. Tickets are priced at one yuan each. Season tickets and complimentary tickets will not be valid. It is also reported that in any competition held at the French Club grounds in previous years, the French Club would typically receive 40% of the ticket revenue. This time, they have voluntarily waived this, demonstrating the deep sorrow and sympathy for Mr. Qiu from both Chinese and foreign individuals. All matches, such as the senior grass court semi-final and the Roper Cup final, will be played in a best-of-five-sets format, while the special exhibition match by Lin Ka will be in a best-of-three-sets format. The order is as follows:

(1) Corassa vs. the winner between Ma Anquan and Forbes (Senior Singles Semi-Final)

(2) Defore and Bonaventure (England) vs. Carson and Squires (USA) (Roper Cup Doubles Final)

(3) Lin Baohua vs. Carson (Senior Singles Semi-Final)

Cup Donation to Begin Next Week

In addition, Mr. Hu Yisheng, a veteran of tennis, initiated a donation drive for the Feihai Memorial Cup due to Mr. Qiu's great contribution to the Chinese tennis community. It has been decided that the drive will begin next Monday. The donation collection point is the Xinhua Trust & Savings Bank branch at 500 Avenue Joffre, at the intersection of Rue Hua Long. Mr. Chen Bugao, the manager of the branch, has always admired Mr. Qiu's skills and morality. His voluntary service this time is commendable. From the donations received, over two hundred yuan will be used to purchase the memorial cup, and the remaining amount will be remitted to Mr. Qiu's family.

Lawn Tennis, All Groups Enter Semi-Finals

After the weekend's competitions in lawn tennis, Lin Baohua defeated Masure in straight sets in the second division of the senior singles. Although Carson narrowly defeated his old partner Squires by two to one, he was constantly threatened by Squires and barely avoided defeat, which was very fortunate. Corassa, who had a bye, also won against Judickson by three to zero. Currently, in the semi-finals during the week, Carson, Lin Baohua, and Corassa have already advanced. Only the Ma Anquan vs. Forbes group has not yet been resolved. The Lin Ka semi-final has been scheduled to be held at the French Club on Saturday. This match was originally intended to be a Qiu Feihai memorial match, but it has now been canceled because the memorial match has been rescheduled to Sunday. At that time, Lin Ka will perform another special exhibition. In the open doubles, Masure and Masters defeated Kimura and Uchida in the first week. The second week was taken by Carson and Squires. Lin Baohua and Deford also defeated Phelps and Pantitat in the first week. Since the beginning of the tournament, only He Jiajian and Liu Zeng have entered the second week, with very few others having advanced. In the junior singles, in addition to Xu Demin, Hu Xuguang, and Luo Minmo, who have secured spots in the semi-finals, Zhao Junzhao was defeated by Land Slingeck the day before yesterday. Land was then defeated by Masters in the third week. Currently, the semi-final spot has been secured by Masters, who will face Xu Demin. Masters has been in excellent form recently and is often a strong opponent for Xu in the semi-finals.
